Hi Josh

As I suggested in our chat yesterday, I believe it is only right that the Audit Squad still has access (as a priority) to one full-time equivalent developer at all times. I do not think having access, as a guarantee, to only half a sprint-worth of time will be sufficient in general.

We will, of course,  try to plan sufficiently to cover that time, and it may well be that we do not have a full sprint-worth of planned work a significant amount of the time, and the developer's time can be used elsewhere when that is the case.

However, a significant amount of time is of an ad hoc nature, particularly when it comes to supporting client issues. In order for us to continue to provide a good service to our clients it is essential that we have that resource available as a priority.

We are very keen to support the Financials team through their current resource challenges, but this mustn't be at the expense of our service to our significant number of Audit app users.

Looking ahead we do have a number of projects that are likely to involve significant developer resource. Immediately, we have the issue of the synced TB not working correctly with our sampling forms (which only came to light last week), in the medium term we are being asked about the analysis schedules on Charity and Academy (which will require specifying and developer resource), and I also have changes to the B30/B31 planned (although this is more remote as it requires platform changes as well, which isn't in my control timing-wise).

I fully understand the really difficult situation you are trying to manage at the moment, and, as I said, you do have our support with that, and hopefully the resource gaps can be filled quickly with the new recruits bedding in and getting up and running in good time.

## [TO/CC] 2026-02-09 16:09 | Cloud Audit & Patrick 
**Folder:** \\liam.bond@caseware.com\Deleted Items

```
Hi all,

I wanted to put this in writing, so we have a clear reference point going forward.

With the recent staffing changes in Development, Will Walker will need to be more directly involved with Cloud Financials to ensure upcoming product releases stay on track.

As a result, there is a gap within Cloud Audit that Patrick will cover on a part‑time basis, which should be manageable given the current workload.
Following discussions with Joe, our plan is for Patrick to dedicate at least the first week of each 2‑week sprint to Cloud Audit, with the second week focused on Submissions, Trackers, and other related work.

There may occasionally be situations, such as last week, where Audit requires additional support for a hotfix or urgent issue. However, these should be exceptions rather than the standard cadence.

Patrick has also been asked to provide Joe with regular updates on his workload and to flag any inefficiencies so we can ensure his time is used effectively.

Given this setup, it is essential that Audit development work is planned and specified well in advance. Workload prioritisation should focus on necessary compliance changes and critical bug fixes, with reduced emphasis on lower‑priority “nice to have” items.

Happy to discuss further if needed.

Thanks,

Josh Sullivan
Software Development Manager

## [TO/CC] 2025-11-21 15:02 | HAT Desktop and Cloud releases
**Folder:** \\liam.bond@caseware.com\Deleted Items

```
Hi Andrew and Getrude

Just a note to keep you in the loop on the Desktop and Cloud releases.

We have finished the checks on the Desktop HAT Working Papers Template, and that is set for release on Thursday next week.

On the Cloud template, we have switched on the Group and Central Planning features that you saw being demo'd at CwX. That is on the version on the Develop server, so you can have a look at that on there right now if you want.

You select the Group Audit by clicking on the Entity name in the top corner and then selecting it from the dropdown at the bottom of the dialog

You can choose in the template Settings whether you want "Group audit" or "Consolidation" to appear first.

However, enabling Groups means that Will has had to do some extra work on the sampling forms to ensure that they pick up the correct TB values.

Notably, in the Group situation, using Parent Materiality and TB values should no longer be an option. That is because the top layer in a Group Audit scenario will always be the Consolidated figures for the Group as a whole, with the Parent being classed as a Component.

Parent Materiality is only really a concept in the Consolidation file scenario where you have separate group and Parent Materiality figures in the Materiality document.

We are in the process of adding that to the file and should have it available for you to give the once over early next week. Once that is done we can push it to the Release server later next week and then to Production servers the following week.

Jonathan Millar
Audit Product Manager
jonathan.millar@caseware.com <mailto:jonathan.millar@caseware.com>

## [TO/CC] 2025-08-15 17:28 | Re: Embedded data analytics workflow proposal in UK Cloud Audit apps
**Folder:** \\liam.bond@caseware.com\Deleted Items

```
Hi all,

This is an area we'd need to discuss directly.

We support the schemas Edison presented, but the import workflow for these is not what it needs to be. Our understanding is that to have an effective experience, we'd need greater validation specific to these import types as well as some level of data preparation tooling.

Users would have to manually cleanse the data in-advance to importing it, assuming they have the relevant subledgers in Excel format.

The biggest opportunity to effectively support these datasets is through direct connectors - e.g. out of the box connectors or Validis. As these wouldn't require any manual data prep. That being said, we've had limited rollout of non-GL analytic tests within the platform (primarily DAS that has enabled these) — and imports for and tests on these datasets are less battle-tested.

We do not currently have plans to support bank transactions or other schemas in the FY roadmap, but should discuss if the opportunity is significant. We will need to consider the e2e workflow holistically, thanks Edison for framing this in his prior messaging.

Please let me know if you'd like to discuss more directly, or how to best engage on this.

Thanks,
Quinn

Quinn Daneyko
​​​​
Senior Product Manager

Subledger dataset

Description

Accounts payable - invoices <https://can01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdocs.caseware.com%2F2020%2Fwebapps%2F31%2Fen%2FEngagements%2FFile-Preparation%2FSubledger-data-schema-AP-invoices.htm&data=05%7C02%7Cliam.bond%40caseware.com%7Cd40f2c8a77c14885da4e08dddc03ffeb%7C7b8a41e42f764eef87d3f75dd19c0e56%7C0%7C0%7C638908631928581897%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=E50fh3Vr0ZqhdlcwSt3XbgmW3JbG%2BlyfMAUL7IqqVIU%3D&reserved=0>

🚨 Evacuation Procedure Reminder:
In the event of a fire or emergency:

1.	Stay calm and leave your belongings behind.
2.	Follow the green emergency exit signs to the nearest safe exit these can be found at either end of the office (the main entrance door and the backdoor)
3.	Do not use lifts during evacuation.
4.	
	Proceed to the designated assembly point outside the building in the car park against the back wall .
5.	
	Wait for further instructions from a Fire Marshal or emergency services before re-entering the building.

	Please see the evacuation plan attached. 
	
	

🎥  AV Room Emergency Pull Cord:

*	
	    The AV room is a sound proof room and therefore has been fitted with an emergency pull cord. This cord needs to reach the floor so please do not tie this up, this is to be pulled in case of an                 emergency, it will sound a high pitched alarm (different to the fire alarm). 
*	
	    On hearing this alarm please check the room for any problems.

If you have any questions or need further clarification, feel free to reach out.
Thanks for helping us keep the workplace safe!

## [TO/CC] 2025-08-04 15:02 | Re: MKS actions for support
**Folder:** \\liam.bond@caseware.com\Sent Items

```
Hi Ricky, John,

We have implemented several fixes on our end to prevent the generation of null repeaters, which have been causing issues on B30 and B31. Currently, the resolution from the CWI side is scheduled for release in August 2025, as noted in the flat ticket [FLAT-11808] "Null" Repeaters Causing Significant Issues on Tables/Forms Using LinkedRepeatForm - Caseware Jira. <https://caseware.atlassian.net/browse/FLAT-11808> 

We will need to monitor the situation to determine if we should remove or adjust our preventative measures. Since CWI's fix is expected to eliminate the error entirely, our interim solutions may need adjustment. We will check this during the beta period.
